  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_14bbc924-24be-4155-82f9-ab3dd0b6ea58'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer15446024649114956624">Two years ago Trotter saved the entire pantheon of Realm from a dark god’s revenge. Unfortunately, that didn’t stop the gods from banning her from Realm and - worst of all - from her godly parents for refusing to honor the Accord and declare her dominion. Now even her refuge in Aevum has been destroyed as the world itself is violently tilted and plunged into darkness. Angr</span>
  <span id="freeText15446024649114956624" style="display:none">Two years ago Trotter saved the entire pantheon of Realm from a dark god’s revenge. Unfortunately, that didn’t stop the gods from banning her from Realm and - worst of all - from her godly parents for refusing to honor the Accord and declare her dominion. Now even her refuge in Aevum has been destroyed as the world itself is violently tilted and plunged into darkness. Angry, tired of feeling helpless and even more tired of being told not to meddle in the affairs of mortals, she’s ready to battle whatever demons she might find behind this nightmare. Instead of evil, however, she discovers another world even older than Aevum and filled with a wonderful species of people the gods created and loved briefly, then abandoned and left for dead in favor of their more entertaining creation: humanity. <br /><br />In order to save both of the worlds she’s come to love, Trotter will finally be forced to choose a dominion that might mean giving up one world permanently. Yet throughout her journey she is unaware that the terrifying darkness growing within her is an omen that another dominion has already chosen her…</span>
  <a data-text-id="15446024649114956624" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2312833786" />

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2312833786?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bobbi Wagner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bobbi Wagner" href="/user/show/59956486-bobbi-wagner">Bobbi Wagner</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2312833786" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16596522130867800880">Tilt: Dreams of Chaos Book 2 by Ashley Chappell is the second book in her Dreams of Chaos series. I highly suggest you read the first book in this series first before this one. You will get background information, story line and enjoy the series better. I enjoyed the first book and I enjoyed the second book just as much. This story is easy flowing and engaging. It is wrote in a way that made me feel as if I was right there with the characters. In this book, Trotter is banished from Realm where s</span>
  <span id="freeText16596522130867800880" style="display:none">Tilt: Dreams of Chaos Book 2 by Ashley Chappell is the second book in her Dreams of Chaos series. I highly suggest you read the first book in this series first before this one. You will get background information, story line and enjoy the series better. I enjoyed the first book and I enjoyed the second book just as much. This story is easy flowing and engaging. It is wrote in a way that made me feel as if I was right there with the characters. In this book, Trotter is banished from Realm where she has been forced to live away from her parents after she refused to chose a domination. She refuses to let politics tell her what to do. Now Aevum is starting to tilt toward eternal darkness. Trotter is left with trying to figure out the cause but with two worlds up heaved, will she finally have to decide a domination? She is unaware of the evil growing within her that just may make her choice easier. Will she lose one of the worlds forever even if it means saving one of them? I enjoyed Trotter in the first adventure and here again in this one she is the heroine. I enjoyed how we got to see a little bit more of inside Trotter's head. She has a need to prove herself but she is a better person for it. There is no doubt that she takes on an adventure through gods, goddesses, mystical creatures that will leave you sitting on the edge of your seat in parts. I love how that Trotter is not your typical character, I think that it adds to the story and to her character. The secondary characters in this book are just as enjoyable. Some you will see from the first book but there are quite a few new ones in this one too. They all just add to the adventure. I highly recommend this book. Find out what adventure Trotter takes us on this time.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2337675339" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11057891784160043691">Tilt (Dreams of Chaos #2) by Ashley Chappell was an action packed, beautifully crafted story that carried over all the elements I loved from the first book. <br/><br/>I love this series, it's original, and when I say original, I mean this plot has not been replicated in anything I have read. From the rich, outstanding world building to the exponential character growth, this book was top tear. It's been a long time since I've read a series, that managed to outdo itself. The first book was amazing, but this</span>
  <span id="freeText11057891784160043691" style="display:none">Tilt (Dreams of Chaos #2) by Ashley Chappell was an action packed, beautifully crafted story that carried over all the elements I loved from the first book. <br /><br />I love this series, it's original, and when I say original, I mean this plot has not been replicated in anything I have read. From the rich, outstanding world building to the exponential character growth, this book was top tear. It's been a long time since I've read a series, that managed to outdo itself. The first book was amazing, but this one.. I can't even being to tell how out-of-this-world good this book is. I want to tell you everything, but I make it a point to not get into a second or third book in a series, because it will spoil the first book. I want you to have the full experience I had so, no spoilers. <br /><br />What I want to stress is that, this series is worth your time, and you will not be able to tare yourself away from it. It's engaging, fresh, with hints of heart brake with a touch of bittersweetness that clashes together to give you an authentic experience like no other. <br /><br />If you haven't gusseted, I highly recommend you not only this book, but this series. I promise that you will not be disappointed. This series will set a new standard of reading for you, and believe me, you will have a hard time trying to find anything that will come close to topping it. <br /><br />Happy Reading <br /><br />-<i>E.A. Walsh</i></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer14708150782618989975">4 Stars<br/><br/>Tilt is the second book in the Dreams of Chaos series by Ashley Chappell. It is a Young Adult fantasy packed with action, adventure, mythology, magic, gods, mystical creatures, different realms/worlds… and so much more.<br/>The story picks up about two years after the previous book. Trotter still hasn’t found where she truly belongs. She’s angry and frustrated after having been banned from Realm for refusing to choose her dominion. Aevum and the world is plunged into darkness as the earth is t</span>
  <span id="freeText14708150782618989975" style="display:none">4 Stars<br /><br />Tilt is the second book in the Dreams of Chaos series by Ashley Chappell. It is a Young Adult fantasy packed with action, adventure, mythology, magic, gods, mystical creatures, different realms/worlds… and so much more.<br />The story picks up about two years after the previous book. Trotter still hasn’t found where she truly belongs. She’s angry and frustrated after having been banned from Realm for refusing to choose her dominion. Aevum and the world is plunged into darkness as the earth is tilted off it’s axis. It looks like it may be up to Trotter to save the day, once again. She certainly gets more than she bargained for on this adventure though, when she discovers a new world. <br />But there is more at play here, and Trotter will have quite a lot to deal with- both internally as well as externally.<br />This story is a little bit darker and more mature than the first book, which I really like. Again, Ms. Chappell did a great job creating a rich and unique world(s), and building wonderful backstory, myths and in-depth lore around this imaginative tale. <br />The character development is quite good, the story abounds with interesting, unique and quirky characters. <br />I look forward to more from Ms. Chappell.<br /><br />Thank you, Ms. Chappell!<br /></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11873433112927199767">Tilt was such a fantastic read! It was even better than Alice Will! It was clear that this book was intended for an older audience as it tackles darker elements of human nature. I enjoyed Trotter's growth in the book. She embraced being a young woman as well as coming into her destiny as a goddess. The balance isn't easy for her as she encounters more dark secrets from the other gods. On to the next!</span>

          </span>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review2368805839">

  <span id="freeText1874115250818668338" style="display:none">I loved Tilt. After reading Alice Will, I knew Ashley Chappell was a fantastic story teller, but the way she continued Trotter's journey was engaging and exciting. <div id="review_2347054360" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2347054360" />
    <a title="Francis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/54382616-francis"><img alt="Francis" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/images/nophoto/user/c_111x148.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2347054360?book_show_action=true">Apr 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Francis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Francis" href="/user/show/54382616-francis">Francis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2347054360" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14692419796080153836">I adored Alice Will, the first book in Ashley Chappell's Dreams of Chaos series, so I was very excited to read Tilt, the sequel. It is another great book! I was instantly drawn into the story and totally engaged and entertained throughout.<br/><br/>It's set a few years after the events of Alice Will, and despite her literally world altering powers Trotter is living a fairly secluded life. She doesn't have complete control over her powers and is scared of this. Trotter has to learn how to reign in her impu</span>
  <span id="freeText14692419796080153836" style="display:none">I adored Alice Will, the first book in Ashley Chappell's Dreams of Chaos series, so I was very excited to read Tilt, the sequel. It is another great book! I was instantly drawn into the story and totally engaged and entertained throughout.<br /><br />It's set a few years after the events of Alice Will, and despite her literally world altering powers Trotter is living a fairly secluded life. She doesn't have complete control over her powers and is scared of this. Trotter has to learn how to reign in her impulses, and acknowledge that even when her intentions are good using her powers is not necessarily the right course of action.<br /><br />We re-encounter many familiar characters, but there's a fair cast of new characters introduced as well. One of my favourites is(/are?) Erwin. The Erwins remind me of the Caterpillar and Cheshire Cat of Alice in Wonderland. They help Trotter figure things out by interpreting things through their own particular logic and understanding of the universe. I love their clever manipulation of words, and also how the other characters react to them (especially poor Prowler!).<br /><br />Chappell's worldbuilding is fantastic - I have such a clear mental image of the places she describes and am fascinated by how everything works and fits together. In Tilt we get to glimpse even more of the beautifully complex universe she has created. With Trotter's ability to move between worlds - from a medievalish market town to the Canvas upon which it is built, and the narrative switching to show us what's going on elsewhere, we really are treated to a huge variety of small worlds, each with their own rules, problems and potentials. The ways they are connected, as well as Chappell's gifts for establishing the character and nature of a place, makes it fairly easy to follow.<br /><br />Tilt is another five star read - a truly excellent book and one I will definitely be recommending to fantasy-loving friends. It is definitely worth starting with Alice Will, both because it is a great book and because it does so much in establishing the characters and setting.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14692419796080153836" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16358042580790241870">a great read about things not being the way you think. when a serious of mysterious events occurs, Trotter believes it is just the actions of the gods. when the sun and moon disappear from Aevum and cause tidal waves, she sets out to reprimand the gods and fix things. but when she discovers it wasn't due to the gods and the sun has been taken elsewhere, she discovers there is more to her world than she thought. pursuing this quest to find answers and punish the man responsible, she soon discover</span>
  <span id="freeText16358042580790241870" style="display:none">a great read about things not being the way you think. when a serious of mysterious events occurs, Trotter believes it is just the actions of the gods. when the sun and moon disappear from Aevum and cause tidal waves, she sets out to reprimand the gods and fix things. but when she discovers it wasn't due to the gods and the sun has been taken elsewhere, she discovers there is more to her world than she thought. pursuing this quest to find answers and punish the man responsible, she soon discovers things will not go the way she expects.a great read. a great example of a sequel adding more to the story and keeping true to the first novel. well developed plot with twists and turns that I just couldn't put down. well developed characters such as Crane with his strengths but also his pain underneath or Trotter struggling with everything but still trying to look after everyone. Miskarot was a great addition with her wise woman nature the plot needed. the Erwin's were also a brilliant addition to add humour. <br />a brilliant novel with stunning visual detail throughout. the use of contrasts with dark and light was beautifully done. I adored the descriptions of Noevum and the mushrooms and the white stones. the contrast in colour with the flames and green fruits was beautifully done. the opposites of life and death were also excellently written. I also loved the descriptions of Red with his shimmering feathers which were spell binding and also added to the worldbuilding with new creatures. the wedge characters were also a brilliant depiction of species of fairies and trolls. overall, a brilliant read and I would give it five stars.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5509234525604300108">Tilt is the second book in the Dreams of Chaos series. Even though you can pick up this book and read it without necessarily reading the first book, I highly recommend getting the first book anyway. I fell in love with the first book almost immediately, and Tilt is just as wonderful. There is a stunning array of colorful characters to both love and hate. Where the first book introduced concepts of how powerful our mind’s creative ability can be, Tilt deals with the struggle of learning how to pr</span>
  <span id="freeText5509234525604300108" style="display:none">Tilt is the second book in the Dreams of Chaos series. Even though you can pick up this book and read it without necessarily reading the first book, I highly recommend getting the first book anyway. I fell in love with the first book almost immediately, and Tilt is just as wonderful. There is a stunning array of colorful characters to both love and hate. Where the first book introduced concepts of how powerful our mind’s creative ability can be, Tilt deals with the struggle of learning how to properly use your power without losing yourself. I cannot recommend these books enough.<br /><br />Trotter, the daughter of gods, is seeing her world change right before her eyes. The days are becoming shorter and the tides are out of synch. Having been forbidden to stay in Realm, home of the gods, Trotter is on her own trying to figure out what is happening. She soon discovers the gods forgotten creation and is thrown into a new world. Even as her own home is being destroyed, Trotter finds that the world she has discovered is also in danger. Trotter has to make a decision that she avoided making in the first book, and it will change everything…even her. A new power is growing within Trotter, but is it something that will be even more dangerous than what they are already facing?<br /><br />Tilt has action, adventure, bravery, gods and monsters, friendship, a bit of romance, and a lot of life lessons. I love the new additions to the cast of characters, especially Erwin. Superior humor is a must when dealing with monsters invading the land. Get the book. Read the book. You will not be disappointed!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16530335156911967933">Tilt: Dreams of Chaos Book 2<br/>By: Ashley Chappell<br/>5 out of 5 stars<br/><br/>The story Tilt: Dreams of Chaos Book 2 by Ashley Chappell is next exciting book in the Dreams of Chaos fantasy series. It continues the story of Trotter and picks up two years after she had saved her world and the Realm, a place that she is currently banned from. Trotter now finds that two worlds, one of which she has always called home, are in danger. Both worlds need help in order to survive. Will Trotter be able to save them both?</span>
  <span id="freeText16530335156911967933" style="display:none">Tilt: Dreams of Chaos Book 2<br />By: Ashley Chappell<br />5 out of 5 stars<br /><br />The story Tilt: Dreams of Chaos Book 2 by Ashley Chappell is next exciting book in the Dreams of Chaos fantasy series. It continues the story of Trotter and picks up two years after she had saved her world and the Realm, a place that she is currently banned from. Trotter now finds that two worlds, one of which she has always called home, are in danger. Both worlds need help in order to survive. Will Trotter be able to save them both? I enjoyed reading this book just as much as the first. It has plenty of action and danger seems to be lurking around every corner. I felt bad for Trotter as she is still trying to get used to the new powers that she has and is also faced with making decisions that affect not only her but those in both the worlds that are in danger. She is finding out that making the rights decisions can be hard. I liked that Trotter is a compassionate person and cares what happens to others. She doesn’t want anyone to be harmed. This story includes characters that you have met in the first book as well as introducing new ones. It is wonderful to read about the strength and determination that is shown by many while they are facing danger. The story goes back and forth between each world and what is happening there. This is a fast-paced book that I had a hard time putting down until I had read the last page. I highly recommend reading the series in order. I can’t wait to read the next book in the series. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16530335156911967933" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2313398217" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9609949105104279679">Tilt by Ashley Chappell is the second in her Dreams of Chaos series and it doesn’t disappoint. It has been two years since Trotter saved her world and the gods themselves from the wrath of a dark god and what did she get out of it, banishment because she refused to play politics and choose a dominion. Now her new home is thrown into eternal night and a new world is discovered, one filled with the procurer race to humanity that the gods abandoned centuries ago. It is in this world that Trotter wi</span>
  <span id="freeText9609949105104279679" style="display:none">Tilt by Ashley Chappell is the second in her Dreams of Chaos series and it doesn’t disappoint. It has been two years since Trotter saved her world and the gods themselves from the wrath of a dark god and what did she get out of it, banishment because she refused to play politics and choose a dominion. Now her new home is thrown into eternal night and a new world is discovered, one filled with the procurer race to humanity that the gods abandoned centuries ago. It is in this world that Trotter will be forced to make decisions that affect not only her but an entire world. With new friends and a few familiar faces Trotter will discover who she is, who she is meant to be, and finally choose a dominion. <br />This book was just as good as the last one. Watching Trotter grow as a character was an amazing experience. Ms. Chappell once again does a fantastic job of creating a world for Trotter, and by extension the readers, to explore. The plot was tightly written and the characters were well developed and relatable. I liked that there was a little bit of romance thrown into this tale as well. It helps to show that for all her power and maturity Trotter is still very much a 16 year old girl. Definitely a four star novel and I am looking forward to reading book three in the series when I get the chance.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9609949105104279679" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText18441021233721180038" style="display:none">Tilt by Ashley Chappell is the second instalment of her Dreams of Chaos series. Not intended as a stand-alone the first book should ideally be read to fully enjoy book two as it follows the same character, follows on from her story in the previous book and builds on what we have already seen.<br /><br />Trotter, despite having saved the world, has been banished. Two years later and she is still living in a home away from home. Settled and continuing on with her life everything is suddenly thrown into chaos when the world when is living on is thrown into darkness.<br />Yet again on a mission to save her home Trotter sets off to find out how to stop the eternal darkness. But with things going on that she is not aware of, it may not be quite that simple.<br /><br />This was a brilliant follow up to a great first book. The writing style had clearly progressed and it made for even better reading. I loved that it wasn’t all sunshine and roses for Trotter despite her having saved everyone. I loved that we got to see her put to the test again as to see her in action.<br />I am looking forward to seeing what else this author has to offer.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5003964758993303643">I give Tilt: Dreams of Chaos Book 2 by Ashley Chappell, 5 stars.<br/>*This review may contain spoilers from book 1.*<br/><br/>Ms Chappell has hit another one out of the park with this book!   <span id="freeText5003964758993303643" style="display:none">I give Tilt: Dreams of Chaos Book 2 by Ashley Chappell, 5 stars.<br />*This review may contain spoilers from book 1.*<br /><br />Ms Chappell has hit another one out of the park with this book! The wonderful young adult fantasy story-telling you loved from book one is back again. So are Trotter and her small but loyal group of friends. But this time it's a completely new problem. Not to mention Trotter trying to figure out her new powers.<br /><br />The cast in this book is so great. Trotter is a wonderful main character, and most of the others are back too, although they do make some more friends and allies along the way. Prowler is also back, which I love, and we are introduced to Erwin, who I hope to see more of!<br /><br />This book is so well written! The story itself is just amazing, but it does not take itself too seriously either. With the opening line of: "Nothing will feed insomnia like accidently turning your own bed into a man-eating beast in your sleep," I knew I was in for another enjoyable wild ride of fun and adventure. <br /><br />Written for Young Adult, this book is definitely for adults also. I could not put it down and highly recommend it to anyone who like a great fantasy!</span>

  <span id="freeText18431581893253361684" style="display:none">Tilt By Ashley Chappell<br /><br />5 Stars!!!!<br /><br /><br /> I like to divert to a different genre every once in a while and this was just the book to break up my constant genre read.   <span id="freeText6083911892136521315" style="display:none">Just as exciting as the first book! It is absolutely necessary to read Alice Will first to get the full scope of what is happening in this book.<br />Trotter saved the world but because of petty politics and refusing to be forced to choose a dominion, she has been banished to Aevum. As she begins to love her new home, it too is thrown into chaos as the whole world begins to tilt and is plunged into endless night. Trotter immediately jump into action to do what she can to save her new home but she may be forced into a dominion after all.<br />I was very excited to read the second book in this series and while I do miss some of the characters from the previous book, this one has so many to love as well. Trotter is still as fierce as ever and as unyielding as she can be when it comes to her morals and I applaud her for that. <br />Ashley Chappell has created a wonderful world and an amazing coming of age story with a tough as nails female lead and I would recommend this series to anyone.</span>

  <span id="freeText9741611858465658762" style="display:none">Tilt- Ashley Chappell<br /><br />4-star review<br /><br />Tilt is another page-turning fantasy read by Ashley Chappell.   <span id="freeText15369900642363997084" style="display:none">Tilt: Dreams of Chaos Book 2 by Ashley Chappell is a wonderfully told imaginative story.   function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('M/oyntyspb8aeX3ZyPlyqShxQozazZ+kFLyNhir9IjDy104Rvb7R4Pc+daltwnyYqTgLxDHltekbYY+Qd3BgQA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }
